–ò–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–µ—Å–Ω–æ–µ –∑–∞–¥–∞–Ω–∏–µ –≤ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–º –∫—É—Ä—Å–∞—á–µ –ø–æ–ø–∞–ª–æ—Å—å, –≤–ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–µ –≤ –∂–∏–∑–Ω–∏ —Å–æ—Ä—Ç–∏—Ä—É—é —Å–ª–æ–≤–∞—Ä—å –ø—É–∑—ã—Ä—å–∫–æ–º
List <Student> Exercise::sort (List <Student> unit) const {
    List <Student> result;
    std::map <Student, int> good, normal, bad;
    for (int i = 0; i < unit.length(); ++i) {
        List <grade> grades = unit[i].getGrades();
        int five = 0, four = 0, three = 0, two = 0;
        for (int j = 0; j < grades.length(); ++j) {
            if (grades[j].mark == 5) {
                ++five;
            }
            else if (grades[j].mark == 4) {
                ++four;
            }
            else if (grades[j].mark == 3) {
                ++three;
            }
            else {
                ++two;
            }
        }
        if (two != 0) {
            bad[unit[i]] = three;
        }
        else if (three != 0) {
            normal[unit[i]] = four;
        }
        else if (four != 0) {
            good[unit[i]] = five;
        }
        else {
           result.append(unit[i]);
        }
    }
    this->sortMap(bad);
    for (std::map<Student, int>::iterator it = bad.begin(); it != bad.end(); ++it) {
        result.append(it->first);
    }
    this->sortMap(normal);
    for (std::map<Student, int>::iterator it = normal.begin(); it != normal.end(); ++it) {
        result.append(it->first);
    }
    this->sortMap(good);
    for (std::map<Student, int>::iterator it = good.begin(); it != good.end(); ++it) {
        result.append(it->first);
    }
    return result;
}

void Exercise::sortMap (std::map <Student, int>& unit) const {
    std::pair <Student, int>* sortedArr = new std::pair <Student, int>[unit.size()];
    int index = 0;
    for (std::map<Student, int>::iterator it = unit.begin(); it != unit.end(); ++it) {
        sortedArr[index++] = *it;
    }
    for (int i = 0; i < unit.size() - 1; ++i) {
        for (int j = 0; j < unit.size() - i - 1; ++j) {
            if (sortedArr[j].second > sortedArr[j + 1].second) {
                std::pair <Student, int> temp = sortedArr[j];
                sortedArr[j] = sortedArr[j + 1];;
                sortedArr[j + 1] = temp;
            }
        }
    }
    std::map <Student, int> ready;
    for (int i = 0; i < unit.size() - 1; ++i) {
        ready.insert(sortedArr[i]);
    }
    unit = ready;
}

import numpy as np

# Define the transformation matrix A
A = np.array([[1, 0, 2], [0, -1, 1], [1, -1, 2]])

# Define the transformation matrix B
B = np.array([[-1, 1, 0], [2, -1, 1], [1, 0, -1]])

# Calculate A^2
A_squared = np.linalg.matrix_power(A, 2)

# Calculate B^-1
B_inv = np.linalg.inv(B)

# Calculate C = A^2 * B^-1
C = np.dot(A_squared, B_inv)

# Convert to decimal and return as a list
C_decimal = C.tolist()

C_decimal

main —â–∞—Å –≤—ã–≥–ª—è–¥–∏—Ç —Ç–∞–∫
#include "cursework.hpp"

int main() {
    setlocale(LC_ALL, "ru_RU.UTF-8");
    StudentList list;
    ifstream file("students.txt");
    if (!file.is_open()) {
        cout << "–û—à–∏–±–∫–∞ –æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã—Ç–∏—è —Ñ–∞–π–ª–∞." << endl;
        return 1;
    }
    string line;
    while (getline(file, line)) {
        stringstream ss(line);

        string name, initials, birthDate, enrollmentYear, faculty, department, group, studentID, gender;
        ss >> name >> initials >> birthDate >> enrollmentYear >> faculty >> department >> group >> studentID >> gender;

            ss >> grade;
            gradesSession1[subject] = grade;

}

#include <windows.h>

int main() {
    SetConsoleCP(1251);
    SetConsoleOutputCP(1251);
    StudentList list;
    ifstream file("students.txt");
    if (!file.is_open()) {
        cout << "–û—à–∏–±–∫–∞ –æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã—Ç–∏—è —Ñ–∞–π–ª–∞." << endl;
        return 1;
    }

        string name, initials, birthDate, enrollmentYear, faculty, department, group, studentID, gender;
        ss >> name >> initials >> birthDate >> enrollmentYear >> faculty >> department >> group >> studentID >> gender;

        map<string, int> gradesSession1;
        map<string, int> gradesSession2;
        int grade;
        std::string subject;
        while (std::getline(ss, subject, '=')) {
            ss >> grade;
            gradesSession1[subject] = grade;
            if (ss.peek() == ',') {
                ss.ignore();
                ss.ignore();
            } else if (ss.peek() == '|') {
                ss.ignore();
                ss.ignore();
                break;
            }
        }

        while (std::getline(ss, subject, '=')) {
            ss >> grade;
            gradesSession2[subject] = grade;
            if (ss.peek() == ',') {
                ss.ignore();
                ss.ignore();
            }
        }

    list.displayStudentsBySession(sessionChoice);

    return 0;
}
